[30;1m121 | [0m[35m---------------[0m

[30;1m123 | [0m[35mDraw :math:`K` **"live" points** (i.e. particles) from the prior[0m
[30;1m124 | [0m[35m:math:`\pi(\boldsymbol{\Theta})`. At each iteration :math:`i`, remove the live[0m

[30;1m127 | [0m[35m:math:`\mathcal{L}_{i+1} \geq \mathcal{L}_i`. It can be shown through some neat[0m

[30;1m178 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m179 | [0m[35mNested Sampling works thanks to the "magic" of **order statistics**.[0m
[30;1m180 | [0m[35mAt the start of a Nested Sampling run, we sample :math:`K` [0m

[30;1m109 | [0m[35m    \sim H_i \Delta \ln X - H_{i-1} \Delta \ln X [0m

[30;1m78 | [0m[35mSince the the prior volumes compress exponentially, the uncertainty on[0m
[30;1m79 | [0m[35m:math:`N` leads to exponential uncertainty in :math:`X` (and hence[0m
